## Brand Guidelines

### 2013

**Logo Information:**

- The role of the Microsoft brand, visual elements, and logo details.
- Text discussing the headline alignment and height relative to the logo.

**Color Information:**

- Color introduction in the visual identity document.
- Specific mention of core colors for Microsoft brand extensions (e.g., Bing, Xbox).
- Headline examples with color usage for content.
- Core brand colors and lighter/darker tints discussion.

**Typography Information:**

- Typography guidelines, including introduction and page references.

**Imagery Photography:**

- Visual role of imagery and its integration with brand identity elements.
- Illustration guidelines, including simple, geometric, and witty uses.
- Usage of Segoe typesetting for captions and featured article styles.

**Spacing Layout:**

- Grid structure underpinning brand guidelines.

**Brand Voice:**

- Content tone focused on simplicity and user mind engagement.

**Notes:**

- Microsoft Visual Identity Guidelines, July 2013.

### 2012

**Logo Information:**

- The Microsoft visual identity system capitalizes on our next wave of product offerings. It helps us be simple, clear, and direct. It elevates the content that matters most. It creates delightful connections. The Microsoft logo celebrates our heritage and our future. It highlights the role we play in many consumers’ lives today, and the increasing breadth of unexpected and innovative products we are delivering. The identity elements—logo, typography, color, grids, tiles, imagery, and icons—make it easier to create memorable internal and external communications.
- 1 The role of the Microsoft brand 2 Identity system elements 7 Logo 17 Logotype 23 Typography 32 Color 39 Grids 41 Tiles 54 Photography 57 Illustration 59 Icons 61 Putting it all together 70 Showcase
- Logo Aa Microsoft Bing Windows Visual Studio XBOX 1
- Logo Segoe Light Segoe Bold Punchy headline goes here 2
- HR Headline is same height as logo, set in Segoe Light. Headline set in Segoe Light, two units tall. Headline twice logo height.

**Color Information:**

- Our 10 core colors have lighter and darker tints 33
- Powerful color combinations: Light tints to darker ranges.
- Tiles provide a colorful starting point for a conversation. They contain elements for effective communication.

**Typography Information:**

- Print Latin, Greek, Cyrillic Segoe Pro Segoe UI (Win 8 version). Includes specific support for international languages aligning with system principles.

**Imagery Photography:**

- Illustrations tell stories and convey ideas. They are simple and geometric. Use illustration when photography won’t work. Illustrations should be witty but not cartoonish, vector-based art, and never decoration.
- Photography and illustration recommendations to ensure high-quality coherent visual communication.

**Spacing Layout:**

- Keep type aligned with the grid for clarity and precise layout structure.
- The underlying grid brings structure to simplicity. It creates the spaces where we tell our stories.

**Notes:**

- Microsoft visual identity guidelines August 2012
- Showcase: some examples of what’s possible with our visual identity system. What we want people to think.
